\DoxyCodeLine{03479\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ [EXPERIMENTAL]\ Low-\/Level:\ Key/Input\ Ownership}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03480\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ The\ idea\ is\ that\ instead\ of\ "{}eating"{}\ a\ given\ input,\ we\ can\ link\ to\ an\ owner\ id.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03481\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ Ownership\ is\ most\ often\ claimed\ as\ a\ result\ of\ reacting\ to\ a\ press/down\ event\ (but\ occasionally\ may\ be\ claimed\ ahead).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03482\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ Input\ queries\ can\ then\ read\ input\ by\ specifying\ ImGuiKeyOwner\_Any\ (==\ 0),\ ImGuiKeyOwner\_NoOwner\ (==\ -\/1)\ or\ a\ custom\ ID.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03483\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ Legacy\ input\ queries\ (without\ specifying\ an\ owner\ or\ \_Any\ or\ \_None)\ are\ equivalent\ to\ using\ ImGuiKeyOwner\_Any\ (==\ 0).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03484\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ Input\ ownership\ is\ automatically\ released\ on\ the\ frame\ after\ a\ key\ is\ released.\ Therefore:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03485\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ -\/\ for\ ownership\ registration\ happening\ as\ a\ result\ of\ a\ down/press\ event,\ the\ SetKeyOwner()\ call\ may\ be\ done\ once\ (common\ case).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03486\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ -\/\ for\ ownership\ registration\ happening\ ahead\ of\ a\ down/press\ event,\ the\ SetKeyOwner()\ call\ needs\ to\ be\ made\ every\ frame\ (happens\ if\ e.g.\ claiming\ ownership\ on\ hover).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03487\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ SetItemKeyOwner()\ is\ a\ shortcut\ for\ common\ simple\ case.\ A\ custom\ widget\ will\ probably\ want\ to\ call\ SetKeyOwner()\ multiple\ times\ directly\ based\ on\ its\ interaction\ state.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03488\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ This\ is\ marked\ experimental\ because\ not\ all\ widgets\ are\ fully\ honoring\ the\ Set/Test\ idioms.\ We\ will\ need\ to\ move\ forward\ step\ by\ step.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03489\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ Please\ open\ a\ GitHub\ Issue\ to\ submit\ your\ usage\ scenario\ or\ if\ there's\ a\ use\ case\ you\ need\ solved.}}
